The buffet breakfast was at the Sheraton, which is right beside the villas (this property and the Sheraton have the same owners). The breakfast spread was delicious and included a variety of western and Chinese options. The villa we stayed in was super spacious with comfy beds, living area and kitchen. All in all, we had an awesome weekend here and can't wait to come back in the summer so we can enjoy the outdoor pools. :)

msg:For the May Day trip, I wanted to find a place where I could relax and have a relaxing vacation without being crowded. Huzhou should be a popular tourist attraction, and the Moon Hotel is also a place to check in. If you want to avoid the hustle and bustle, then this villa resort hotel is the best choice. Bringing the elderly and children, we can gather together when needed, and at the same time have independent space. The three-bedroom villa meets my needs.
1. Convenient location and convenient parking. We walked to the Moon Hotel and the square, and had breakfast at the Sheraton, which was also very convenient.
2. The room has its own hot spring pool and swimming pool. Because the weather is not very hot, the swimming pool is not used. The hot spring pool is still very convenient. After a day of playing, come back to soak and relieve fatigue. There are many green plants in the villa, and there is a lake in front. The most worrying thing is that there are many insects and mosquitoes. I saw them in the yard, but this is also normal. The villa room is still clean.
3. The housekeeper Leo has a good service. WeChat is available at any time, allowing us to solve many problems without leaving home. I saw some reviews saying that it is inconvenient to order takeout, but I didn‚Äôt encounter it in fact. The takeout will be placed at the front desk and the housekeeper will help bring it in.
4. The Moon Hot Spring is not outdoor, but in a glass house with various pools. Maybe I went there at night, so there were few people and the experience was good. There is a warm water children's area in the middle. The children didn't want to go back after playing. The only regret is that we went there on the last day and didn't have time to bring my parents to experience it.
5. We didn't go to the popular attractions in Huzhou. Considering that my parents would not be too tired, we went to the nearby Taihu Scenic Area and Changxing Datang Tribute Tea House. It was a relief to avoid the crowds on May Day~
